***fluwelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fluwelen.html>fluwelen</a> (18064)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fluweel.html>fluweel</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fluwelen.html>fluwelen</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> velveteen, made of velvet</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> velvety, soft and pleasant like velvet</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fok.html>fok</a> (24963)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">focke</i>, presumably from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">focken</i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fokken.html>fokken</a></i>).
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fok.html>fok</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fokken.html>fokken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fok.html>fokje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A foresail</li>
<li>By comparison, of shape:
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_dialects" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch dialects">Southern</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a nose</li>
<li>the head of a cogwheel</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a pair of glasses</li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The activity or business of breeding (notably of domesticated animals)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fokken.html>fokken</a> (10676)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">focken</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">vocken</i>. Likely related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fuck</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">ficken</i>.
</p>

</p>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to strike</li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:folie.html>Folie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">folia</i>, plural form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">folium</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">leaf, sheet</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The word <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">foelie</i> derives from the same source, but <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> older and entered the language <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> Old French.

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:fondue.html>fondue</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">melted</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">fondre</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to melt</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

***fonetisch.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fonetisch.html>fonetisch</a> (131052)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably borrowed, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">phonetisch</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">phonétique</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fonetisch.html>fonetisch</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>phonetic</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***fontein.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:fontein.html>fontein</a> (9350)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fontein.html>fontein</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fontein.html>fonteinen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fontein.html>fonteintje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A well, spring</li>
<li>A fountain, monumental or small artificial water feature</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The water which springs from one of the above; any water</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:forceps.html>forceps</a> (65146)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:forceps.html>forceps</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:forceps.html>forceps</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:forceps.html>forceps</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">forcipes</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">forcepses</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An instrument used in surgery or medical <a href = vnd.unilang:procedures.html>procedures</a> for grasping and holding <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a>, similar to <a href = vnd.unilang:tongs.html>tongs</a> or pincers.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Although the Latin word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> singular, this word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often treated as a plurale tantum by analogy with names for similar <a href = vnd.unilang:items.html>items</a> such as <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tongs.html>tongs</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">tweezers</i>: <i>this <a href = vnd.unilang:forceps.html>forceps</a></i> or <i>these <a href = vnd.unilang:forceps.html>forceps</a></i> (or <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> <i>pair of <a href = vnd.unilang:forceps.html>forceps</a></i>).
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">pair of <a href = vnd.unilang:forceps.html>forceps</a></span></li></ul>

***forel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:forel.html>forel</a> (15431)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Forelle</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">forhel</i>, older <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">forhen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">forhana</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:forel.html>forel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:forellen.html>forellen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:forel.html>forelletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A trout, <i>Salmo trutta</i>.</li>
<li>One of certain fish of the subfamily Salmoninae, specifically certain members of the genera <i>Salvelinus</i> and <i>Oncorhynchus</i>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">voorn</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:forel.html>forel</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:vissen.html>vissen</a>)</span> zalmachtige zoetwatervis</li></ol>

***foreman.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:foreman.html>foreman</a> (10924)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fore-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">foarman</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voorman.html>voorman</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Vormann</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">formand</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">förman</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">formaður</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:foreman.html>foreman</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">foremen</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">management</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The leader of a work crew.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The member of a <a href = vnd.unilang:jury.html>jury</a> who presides <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> it and speaks on its behalf.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> during the era of slavery</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A black (slave) assistant to the white overseer who managed field hands.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">forepeople</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">foreperson</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">forewoman</span></li></ul>
</body>

***forensisch.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:forensisch.html>forensisch</a> (8937)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:forensisch.html>forensisch</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">forensis</i>, from forum (public square where Roman public legal proceedings <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> place)
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:forensisch.html>forensisch</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>legal, court <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a>, trial <a href = vnd.unilang:halal.html>-</a></li>
<li>especially, forensic, relating to the use of science and technology in the investigation and establishment of <a href = vnd.unilang:facts.html>facts</a> or evidence in a court of law</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:forenzen.html>forenzen</a> (61053)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:forens.html>forens</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:forgotten.html>forgotten</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:forgotten.html>forgotten</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:forgotten.html>forgotten</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Of which knowledge <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a>; which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> no longer remembered.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:forgotten.html>forgotten</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">forgottens</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A person or thing that <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:forgotten.html>forgotten</a>.

***formaldehyde.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:formaldehyde.html>formaldehyde</a> (27674)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:formaldehyde.html>formaldehyde</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">formaldehydes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">organic chemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The simplest aldehyde, H-CHO, a colourless gas that <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> many industrial applications; it dissolves in water to give formol (10%) and formalin.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">H-CHO</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">E240</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">when used as a preservative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, methanal <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">IUPAC name</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">formalin</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">formic acid</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">formol</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">thioformaldehyde</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:formaldehyde.html>formaldehyde</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>  <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>

***formeel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:formeel.html>formeel</a> (8759)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">formulaire</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">formularium</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">form (collection)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, itself from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">formula</i> (diminutive of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:forma.html>forma</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">form, shape</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">-arium</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ary</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The current sense <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Formular</i>.
</p>

</p>
